\subsection{Detailed Description}
Reads a True\+Type file or a True\+Type Collection. The True\+Type spec can be found at the Microsoft. Typography site\+: \href{http://www.microsoft.com/truetype/}{\tt http\+://www.\+microsoft.\+com/truetype/}

\index{determine\+Asc\+Desc@{determine\+Asc\+Desc}!org\+::newdawn\+::slick\+::tools\+::hiero\+::truetype\+::\+T\+T\+F\+File@{org\+::newdawn\+::slick\+::tools\+::hiero\+::truetype\+::\+T\+T\+F\+File}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{determine\+Asc\+Desc()}{determineAscDesc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void org.\+newdawn.\+slick.\+tools.\+hiero.\+truetype.\+T\+T\+F\+File.\+determine\+Asc\+Desc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

Determines the right source for the ascender and descender values. The problem here is that the interpretation of these values is not the same for every font. There doesn\textquotesingle{}t seem to be a uniform definition of an ascender and a descender. In some fonts the hhea values are defined after the Apple interpretation, but not in every font. The same problem is in the O\+S/2 table. F\+OP needs the ascender and descender to determine the baseline so we need values which add up more or less to the \char`\"{}em box\char`\"{}. However, due to accent modifiers a character can grow beyond the em box.

\index{read\+C\+M\+AP@{read\+C\+M\+AP}!org\+::newdawn\+::slick\+::tools\+::hiero\+::truetype\+::\+T\+T\+F\+File@{org\+::newdawn\+::slick\+::tools\+::hiero\+::truetype\+::\+T\+T\+F\+File}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{read\+C\+M\+A\+P()}{readCMAP()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily boolean org.\+newdawn.\+slick.\+tools.\+hiero.\+truetype.\+T\+T\+F\+File.\+read\+C\+M\+AP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_font_file_reader}{Font\+File\+Reader}}}]{in }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) throws I\+O\+Exception\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

Read the cmap table, return false if the table is not present or only unsupported tables are present. Currently only unicode cmaps are supported. Set the unicode\+Index in the T\+T\+F\+Mtx\+Entries and fills in the cmaps vector.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em in} & The reader to get the table from \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the table has been read 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em I\+O\+Exception} & Indicates a failure to read the table \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\begin{DoxyCode}
252                                                                    \{
253 
254         \mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_t_t_f_file_a2c9280bb8fa734f8deb6de981a0b4fea}{unicodeMapping}} = \textcolor{keyword}{new} java.util.ArrayList();
255 
256         \textcolor{comment}{//Read CMAP table and correct mtxTab.index}
257         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mtxPtr = 0;
258 
259         \mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_t_t_f_file_abccbd8b00bcebc8015fa41fef0239cf4}{seekTab}}(in, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"cmap"}, 2);
260         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} numCMap = in.readTTFUShort();    \textcolor{comment}{// Number of cmap subtables}
261         \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} cmapUniOffset = 0;
262 
263         \mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_t_t_f_file_ae6acbd4aea68fd8cf15305aa535993f4}{log}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_log_a7c258286d01348186fadbb45f0da36b9}{info}}(numCMap + \textcolor{stringliteral}{" cmap tables"});
264 
265         \textcolor{comment}{//Read offset for all tables. We are only interested in the unicode table}
266         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < numCMap; i++) \{
267             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cmapPID = in.readTTFUShort();
268             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cmapEID = in.readTTFUShort();
269             \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} cmapOffset = in.readTTFULong();
270 
271             \mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_t_t_f_file_ae6acbd4aea68fd8cf15305aa535993f4}{log}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classorg_1_1newdawn_1_1slick_1_1tools_1_1hiero_1_1truetype_1_1_log_a067b2d2d3d00472e36456a266302dc5b}{debug}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Platform ID: "} + cmapPID + \textcolor{stringliteral}{" Encoding: "} + cmapEID);
272 
273             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (cmapPID == 3 && cmapEID == 1) \{
274                 cmapUniOffset = cmapOffset;
275             \}
276         \}
277
